    <li> As my title suggests, I love this product.  It is great for both relaxed and natural people when used to moisturize hair and seal the ends. I would strongly advise against that. I do not have a sensitive scalp but when I placed this product on my scalp, I experienced terrible itching and raised bumps all over my head. Further research showed that others also experienced this. The itching and the bumps did not go away after one wash. It took maybe two washes for the symptoms to subside. I did, however and unfortunately, notice more growth around my edges where I was using the product on my scalp. I just felt in the end that the pain was not worth it. If you really want to try it on your scalp (because I do know at least one person for whom this product did not cause a negative reaction), I would use the spot treatment method. Apply it to one spot on your scalp and note if you feel any different. Then wait until the next morning before trying it elsewhere on your scalp. I always felt it by the morning.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;With regard to nature of the product itself, firstly,  it does not have a strong smell.     <li> I received the product very timely, almost too quickly...:O)  When I first read about the benefits of JBCO, out of impatience, I drove the same day to a local beauty supply and bought a small bottle (a no-name brand ...lol. Had I known the Amazon shipment would be so quick, I might have waited)...But I digress..  So, I&#x27;m nearly out of the no-name brand and will begin this product shortly.  (Hence the 4 stars versus 5).    MY RESULTS: My edges were never really bad, but due to years of wig-wearing my hairline had become somewhat thin. That was my original reason for using the JBCO. And I have noticed a difference already. At 2 places near my left and right temples, the hair which was noticeably thinner is now filling in.  Yay!  I told a friend about it.  She used it on her daughter&#x27;s edges and they have now filled in as well!    PLEASE KNOW: For those of you ladies who continue to lose hair despite using JBCO, you might also look into OTHER POTENTIAL REASONS.  A few years ago, my hair just started coming out.  Not breaking out, COMING OUT, as I have always had lots of long, thick hair (I mostly wear wigs for variety of style and color). Thank the Lord, my hair also grows fast, otherwise with the amount I lost, I&#x27;d have been bald in not time...:O( Just touching my hair, I would have swatches of my hair in my hand.  Because I had just reached a &#x27;milestone birthday,&#x27;  I attributed it to the natural progression of age.  During a routine annual physical, however, I finally learned I was anemic.  I believe this contributed to my hair loss.  For as soon as I began iron supplements and reversed the anemia, my hair stopped coming out.    Also, hormonal imbalances (especially thyroid imbalance) will definitely cause you to lose hair. (BTW, if you don&#x27;t eat iodized salt or take kelp or seaweed supplements, your iodine intake may be too low. Low iodine negatively affects your thyroid).    So, before you give up, have your doctor or nutritionist check for these common issues we women have.  All the oil in the world won&#x27;t undo the effects of an imbalance in the body.  Believe me, I know.  Being someone who would&#x27;ve tried everything on the market to stop my hair from falling out, I can honestly say JBCO would not have worked on me until I corrected the blood anemia.    Hope this helps those who haven&#x27;t been able to find the answer otherwise.    Blessings!</li>
